<C><I>of Venice</I>.</C>
<L />
<C>{W}ith the extreame cueltie of <I>Shylocke</I> the Iewe</C>
<C>towards the {s}ayd Merchant, in cutting a iu{{s}t} pound</C>
<C>of his {fl}e{{s}h}: and the obtayning of <I>Portia</I></C>
<C>by the choy{s}e of three</C>
<C>che{{s}t}s.</C>
<L />
<C><I>As it hath beene diuers times a{ct}ed by the Lord </I></C>
<C><I>Chamberlaine his Seruants</I>.</C>
